	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cutoff;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _NormalStrong;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _IFMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RenderType;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cull;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _ReflectionColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec3 _ReflectionOffset;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD10;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD11;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD12;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump float u_xlat16_10;
float u_xlat18;
mediump float u_xlat16_22;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _UVScallePaner.xy + _UVScallePaner.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.w = 0.0;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.z = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    vs_TEXCOORD0.z = min(max(vs_TEXCOORD0.z, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    vs_TEXCOORD0.z = clamp(vs_TEXCOORD0.z, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat3.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _MainHighLightOffset.xyz + _LocalLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_22) + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_3;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat5.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat5.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat5.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.xzw = u_xlat16_4.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_10)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_4.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_4.z;
    u_xlat2.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + (-_ReflectionOffset.xyz);
    u_xlat2 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat2 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat2;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat2;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat0.y = u_xlat0.y * _ProjectionParams.x;
    u_xlat2.xzw = u_xlat0.xwy * vec3(0.5, 0.5, 0.5);
    vs_TEXCOORD12.zw = u_xlat0.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD12.xy = u_xlat2.zz + u_xlat2.xw;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat1.x = _Offset * 0.00999999978;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x / u_xlat0.w;
    gl_Position.z = u_xlat0.z + (-u_xlat1.x);
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat0.xyw;
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _ReflectionTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD12;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec2 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
vec3 u_xlat6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_12;
float u_xlat18;
mediump float u_xlat16_28;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _NormalStrong;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_10.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat16_10.xy;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat16_10.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_3.y = dot(u_xlat16_10.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_3.z = dot(u_xlat16_10.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat9.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat9.x = min(max(u_xlat9.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat9.x = clamp(u_xlat9.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18 = (-u_xlat9.x) * u_xlat9.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_2.y + _RoughNessOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_28 = min(max(u_xlat16_28, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_28 = clamp(u_xlat16_28, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat9.x + u_xlat18;
    u_xlat9.x = max(u_xlat9.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat16_3.x / u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat16_28 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat18;
    u_xlat9.x = min(u_xlat9.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_2.x + _MetallicOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_12.x = min(max(u_xlat16_12.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_12.x = clamp(u_xlat16_12.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_4 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = (-u_xlat16_4.xyz) * u_xlat16_12.xxx + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat9.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat9.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat9.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_12.xyz + u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_12.x = dot((-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_12.x + u_xlat16_12.x;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-u_xlat16_12.xxx) + (-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_12.x = (-u_xlat16_28) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_12.x;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_1 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_12.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_12.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_12.x = max(u_xlat16_12.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_12.x = log2(u_xlat16_12.x);
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_12.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_12.x = exp2(u_xlat16_12.x);
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_12.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_12.xxx;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xxx;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * _EnvScale.xyz;
    u_xlat7.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat7.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat7.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat7.xyz + u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_2.w * _IFEmiss;
    u_xlat16_12.x = sqrt(u_xlat16_2.z);
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xxx;
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_4.w + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = _IFMask * u_xlat16_8.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_3.xzw * _EmissColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_12.xxx + u_xlat16_3.xzw;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat2.xy = vs_TEXCOORD12.xy / vs_TEXCOORD12.ww;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_ReflectionTex, u_xlat2.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * _ReflectionColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz / u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(1.01900005, 1.01900005, 1.01900005);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.20000005, 2.20000005, 2.20000005);
    SV_Target0.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    return;
}

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RoughNessOffset;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cutoff;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _NormalStrong;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _IFMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RenderType;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cull;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ZWrite;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ZTest;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _AlphaToMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SrcBlendFactor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DstBlendFactor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SrcBlendFactorAlpha;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DstBlendFactorAlpha;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _BlendOp;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _BlendOpAlpha;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EmissColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MetallicOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _IFEmiss;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _GlobalLightEmiss;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _LocalLightOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _ReflectionColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec3 _ReflectionOffset;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD10;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD11;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD12;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump float u_xlat16_10;
float u_xlat18;
mediump float u_xlat16_22;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _UVScallePaner.xy + _UVScallePaner.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.w = 0.0;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.z = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    vs_TEXCOORD0.z = min(max(vs_TEXCOORD0.z, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    vs_TEXCOORD0.z = clamp(vs_TEXCOORD0.z, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * unity_LightmapST.xy + unity_LightmapST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat3.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _MainHighLightOffset.xyz + _LocalLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_22) + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_3;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat5.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat5.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat5.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.xzw = u_xlat16_4.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_10)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_4.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_4.z;
    u_xlat2.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + (-_ReflectionOffset.xyz);
    u_xlat2 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat2 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat2;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat2;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat0.y = u_xlat0.y * _ProjectionParams.x;
    u_xlat2.xzw = u_xlat0.xwy * vec3(0.5, 0.5, 0.5);
    vs_TEXCOORD12.zw = u_xlat0.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD12.xy = u_xlat2.zz + u_xlat2.xw;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat1.x = _Offset * 0.00999999978;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x / u_xlat0.w;
    gl_Position.z = u_xlat0.z + (-u_xlat1.x);
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat0.xyw;
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _ReflectionTex;

UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D unity_Lightmap;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(5) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD12;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec2 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
vec3 u_xlat6;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_9;
vec3 u_xlat10;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_11;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_13;
mediump float u_xlat16_17;
float u_xlat20;
mediump float u_xlat16_27;
mediump float u_xlat16_31;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _NormalStrong;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_11.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat16_11.xy;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat16_11.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_3.y = dot(u_xlat16_11.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_3.z = dot(u_xlat16_11.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat10.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat10.x = min(max(u_xlat10.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat10.x = clamp(u_xlat10.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat20 = (-u_xlat10.x) * u_xlat10.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_2.y + _RoughNessOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_31 = min(max(u_xlat16_31, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_31 = clamp(u_xlat16_31, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_31 * u_xlat16_31;
    u_xlat10.x = u_xlat10.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat10.x = u_xlat10.x * u_xlat10.x + u_xlat20;
    u_xlat10.x = max(u_xlat10.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat10.x = u_xlat16_3.x / u_xlat10.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat10.x = u_xlat10.x * u_xlat10.x;
    u_xlat20 = u_xlat16_31 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat10.x = u_xlat10.x * u_xlat20;
    u_xlat10.x = min(u_xlat10.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_13.x = u_xlat16_2.x + _MetallicOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_13.x = min(max(u_xlat16_13.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_13.x = clamp(u_xlat16_13.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_4 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_13.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = (-u_xlat16_4.xyz) * u_xlat16_13.xxx + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat10.xyz = u_xlat10.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat10.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat10.xyz;
    u_xlat10.xyz = u_xlat10.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat10.xyz = u_xlat10.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_13.xyz + u_xlat10.xyz;
    u_xlat6.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat6.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat6.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_1.y * 0.5 + 0.75;
    u_xlat16_7.x = max(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_7.x = min(u_xlat16_7.x, 1.25);
    u_xlat16_17 = (-u_xlat16_7.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_6 = texture(unity_Lightmap, vs_TEXCOORD1.xy);
    u_xlat16_27 = u_xlat16_6.w;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(4.84000015, 4.84000015, 4.84000015);
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_27 * u_xlat16_17 + u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = u_xlat16_13.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xxx * u_xlat16_13.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_27) + u_xlat16_13.xyz;
    u_xlat16_13.x = dot((-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_13.x = u_xlat16_13.x + u_xlat16_13.x;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-u_xlat16_13.xxx) + (-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_13.x = (-u_xlat16_31) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_31 * u_xlat16_13.x;
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_31 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_1 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_31);
    u_xlat16_13.x = u_xlat16_1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_13.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_13.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_13.x = max(u_xlat16_13.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_13.x = log2(u_xlat16_13.x);
    u_xlat16_13.x = u_xlat16_13.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_13.x = exp2(u_xlat16_13.x);
    u_xlat16_13.x = u_xlat16_13.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_13.xxx;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_13.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xxx;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * _EnvScale.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_2.w * _IFEmiss;
    u_xlat16_13.x = sqrt(u_xlat16_2.z);
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xxx;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_4.w + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = _IFMask * u_xlat16_7.x + 1.0;

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;

vec4 u_xlat0;

mediump float u_xlat16_22;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _UVScallePaner.xy + _UVScallePaner.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.w = 0.0;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.z = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    vs_TEXCOORD0.z = min(max(vs_TEXCOORD0.z, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    vs_TEXCOORD0.z = clamp(vs_TEXCOORD0.z, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat3.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _MainHighLightOffset.xyz + _LocalLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_22);

    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_3;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat5.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat5.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat5.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.xzw = u_xlat16_4.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_10)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_4.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_4.z;
    u_xlat2.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + (-_ReflectionOffset.xyz);
    u_xlat2 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat2 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat2;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat2;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat0.y = u_xlat0.y * _ProjectionParams.x;
    u_xlat2.xzw = u_xlat0.xwy * vec3(0.5, 0.5, 0.5);
    vs_TEXCOORD12.zw = u_xlat0.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD12.xy = u_xlat2.zz + u_xlat2.xw;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat1.x = _Offset * 0.00999999978;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x / u_xlat0.w;
    gl_Position.z = u_xlat0.z + (-u_xlat1.x);
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat0.xyw;
    return;
}

mediump float u_xlat16_28;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _NormalStrong;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_10.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat16_10.xy;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat16_10.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_3.y = dot(u_xlat16_10.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_3.z = dot(u_xlat16_10.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat9.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat9.x = min(max(u_xlat9.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat9.x = clamp(u_xlat9.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18 = (-u_xlat9.x) * u_xlat9.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_2.y + _RoughNessOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_28 = min(max(u_xlat16_28, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_28 = clamp(u_xlat16_28, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat9.x + u_xlat18;
    u_xlat9.x = max(u_xlat9.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat16_3.x / u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_3.x;

#endif
    u_xlat16_4 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);

    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat9.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat9.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat9.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_12.xyz + u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_12.x = dot((-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_12.x + u_xlat16_12.x;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-u_xlat16_12.xxx) + (-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_12.x = (-u_xlat16_28) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_12.x;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_1 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_12.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_12.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_12.x = max(u_xlat16_12.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_12.x = log2(u_xlat16_12.x);
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_12.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_12.x = exp2(u_xlat16_12.x);
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_12.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_12.xxx;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xxx;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * _EnvScale.xyz;
    u_xlat7.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat7.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat7.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat7.xyz + u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_2.w * _IFEmiss;
    u_xlat16_12.x = sqrt(u_xlat16_2.z);
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xxx;
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_4.w + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = _IFMask * u_xlat16_8.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_3.xzw * _EmissColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_12.xxx + u_xlat16_3.xzw;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat2.xy = vs_TEXCOORD12.xy / vs_TEXCOORD12.ww;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_ReflectionTex, u_xlat2.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * _ReflectionColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.20000005, 2.20000005, 2.20000005);

void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _UVScallePaner.xy + _UVScallePaner.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.w = 0.0;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);

    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_3;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);

in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD1;

out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD12;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec3 u_xlat1;

mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump float u_xlat16_10;
float u_xlat18;
mediump float u_xlat16_22;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _UVScallePaner.xy + _UVScallePaner.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.w = 0.0;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.z = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    vs_TEXCOORD0.z = min(max(vs_TEXCOORD0.z, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    vs_TEXCOORD0.z = clamp(vs_TEXCOORD0.z, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * unity_LightmapST.xy + unity_LightmapST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat3.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _MainHighLightOffset.xyz + _LocalLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_22) + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_3;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat5.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat5.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat5.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.xzw = u_xlat16_4.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_10)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_4.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_4.z;
    u_xlat2.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + (-_ReflectionOffset.xyz);
    u_xlat2 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat2 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat2;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat2;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat0.y = u_xlat0.y * _ProjectionParams.x;
    u_xlat2.xzw = u_xlat0.xwy * vec3(0.5, 0.5, 0.5);
    vs_TEXCOORD12.zw = u_xlat0.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD12.xy = u_xlat2.zz + u_xlat2.xw;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat1.x = _Offset * 0.00999999978;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x / u_xlat0.w;
    gl_Position.z = u_xlat0.z + (-u_xlat1.x);
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat0.xyw;
    return;
}

{
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _NormalStrong;

#endif

    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);

    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;

    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat10.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat10.x = min(max(u_xlat10.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat10.x = clamp(u_xlat10.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat20 = (-u_xlat10.x) * u_xlat10.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_2.y + _RoughNessOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_31 = min(max(u_xlat16_31, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_31 = clamp(u_xlat16_31, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif

    u_xlat10.x = u_xlat10.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat10.x = u_xlat10.x * u_xlat10.x + u_xlat20;
    u_xlat10.x = max(u_xlat10.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat10.x = u_xlat16_3.x / u_xlat10.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat10.x = u_xlat10.x * u_xlat10.x;
    u_xlat20 = u_xlat16_31 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat10.x = u_xlat10.x * u_xlat20;
    u_xlat10.x = min(u_xlat10.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_13.x = u_xlat16_2.x + _MetallicOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_13.x = min(max(u_xlat16_13.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_13.x = clamp(u_xlat16_13.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_4 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);

    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(4.84000015, 4.84000015, 4.84000015);

    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = u_xlat16_13.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xxx * u_xlat16_13.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_27) + u_xlat16_13.xyz;
    u_xlat16_13.x = dot((-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_13.x = u_xlat16_13.x + u_xlat16_13.x;

    u_xlat16_13.x = (-u_xlat16_31) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_31 * u_xlat16_13.x;

uniform 	float _Offset;
uniform 	vec4 _MainLightPosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainLightColor;
uniform 	vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;
uniform 	vec4 _ProjectionParams;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_WorldTransformParams;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[20];
uniform 	mediump vec4 _UVScallePaner;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _LocalLightOffset;
uniform 	vec3 _ReflectionOffset;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _DarkCorner;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainHighLightOffset;
attribute highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
attribute highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
attribute highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
attribute highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
varying mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD10;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD11;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD12;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump float u_xlat16_10;
float u_xlat18;
mediump float u_xlat16_22;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _UVScallePaner.xy + _UVScallePaner.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.w = 0.0;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.z = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD0.z = clamp(vs_TEXCOORD0.z, 0.0, 1.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat3.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat3.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _LocalLightOffset.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_22) + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_3;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat5.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat5.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat5.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.xzw = u_xlat16_4.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_10)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat2.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_4.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_4.z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + (-_ReflectionOffset.xyz);
    u_xlat2 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat2 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat2;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat2;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat0.y = u_xlat0.y * _ProjectionParams.x;
    u_xlat2.xzw = u_xlat0.xwy * vec3(0.5, 0.5, 0.5);
    vs_TEXCOORD12.zw = u_xlat0.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD12.xy = u_xlat2.zz + u_xlat2.xw;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat1.x = _Offset * 0.00999999978;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x / u_xlat0.w;
    gl_Position.z = u_xlat0.z + (-u_xlat1.x);
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat0.xyw;
    return;
}

#ifdef FRAGMENT

#ifdef GL_FRAGMENT_PRECISION_HIGH
    precision highp float;

    precision mediump float;

precision highp int;
uniform 	vec4 _EnvScale;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHAr;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHAg;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHAb;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHBr;

uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHBb;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHC;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainLightShadowParams;
uniform 	mediump float _RoughNessOffset;
uniform 	mediump float _NormalStrong;
uniform 	mediump float _IFMask;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _EmissColor;
uniform 	mediump float _MetallicOffset;

uniform lowp samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;

varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD12;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
#define SV_Target0 gl_FragData[0]
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
lowp vec4 u_xlat10_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
lowp vec4 u_xlat10_2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
lowp vec4 u_xlat10_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
vec3 u_xlat6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
vec3 u_xlat8;
lowp vec3 u_xlat10_8;
bool u_xlatb9;
mediump float u_xlat16_10;
vec3 u_xlat15;
mediump float u_xlat16_19;
float u_xlat24;
mediump float u_xlat16_28;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, vs_TEXCOORD7.xy).x;
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlat0.x<vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
    u_xlat16_1.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 0.0 : _MainLightShadowParams.x;
    u_xlat16_10 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x + u_xlat16_10;
    u_xlatb0 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
    u_xlatb9 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlatb9 || u_xlatb0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_10 = _NormalStrong;
    u_xlat16_10 = clamp(u_xlat16_10, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10_2.xyz = texture2D(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat10_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_10) * u_xlat16_3.xy;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_4.y = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_4.z = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_10 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_10 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_10);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_10) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_0.y * 0.5 + 0.75;
    u_xlat16_10 = max(u_xlat16_10, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_10 = min(u_xlat16_10, 1.25);
    u_xlat16_19 = (-u_xlat16_10) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_19 + u_xlat16_10;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat16_0.y * u_xlat16_0.y;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat16_0.x * u_xlat16_0.x + (-u_xlat16_19);
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_0.yzzx * u_xlat16_0.xyzz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(unity_SHBr, u_xlat16_2);
    u_xlat16_3.y = dot(unity_SHBg, u_xlat16_2);
    u_xlat16_3.z = dot(unity_SHBb, u_xlat16_2);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = unity_SHC.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_19) + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.w = 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(unity_SHAr, u_xlat16_0);
    u_xlat16_4.y = dot(unity_SHAg, u_xlat16_0);
    u_xlat16_4.z = dot(unity_SHAb, u_xlat16_0);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = max(u_xlat16_3.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat10_2 = texture2D(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat10_2.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_19 = clamp(u_xlat16_19, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10_4 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = (-u_xlat10_4.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_19) + u_xlat10_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_10) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat6.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat6.x = clamp(u_xlat6.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat15.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat15.x = clamp(u_xlat15.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat24 = (-u_xlat15.x) * u_xlat15.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat10_2.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_10 = clamp(u_xlat16_10, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_10 * u_xlat16_10;
    u_xlat15.x = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat15.x;
    u_xlat15.x = u_xlat15.x * u_xlat15.x + u_xlat24;
    u_xlat15.x = max(u_xlat15.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat15.x = u_xlat16_28 / u_xlat15.x;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_28 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_28 = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat15.x = u_xlat15.x * u_xlat15.x;
    u_xlat24 = u_xlat16_10 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat15.x = u_xlat15.x * u_xlat24;
    u_xlat15.x = min(u_xlat15.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat10_4.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_19) * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat15.xyz = u_xlat15.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat15.xyz = u_xlat6.xxx * u_xlat15.xyz;
    u_xlat15.xyz = u_xlat15.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat15.xyz = u_xlat15.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat15.xyz;
    u_xlat8.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat8.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat8.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xxx + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot((-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz), u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x + u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * (-u_xlat16_1.xxx) + (-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = (-u_xlat16_10) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_10;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * 6.0;
    u_xlat10_0 = textureCube(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat10_0.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_1.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_1.x = log2(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_1.x = exp2(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xxx;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat8.xyz * _EnvScale.xyz + u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat10_2.w * _IFEmiss;
    u_xlat16_10 = sqrt(u_xlat10_2.z);
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = u_xlat10_4.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xxx;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat10_4.w + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = _IFMask * u_xlat16_3.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = u_xlat16_1.xzw * _EmissColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_10) + u_xlat16_1.xzw;
    u_xlat6.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat6.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat6.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat8.xy = vs_TEXCOORD12.xy / vs_TEXCOORD12.ww;
    u_xlat10_8.xyz = texture2D(_ReflectionTex, u_xlat8.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat10_8.xyz * _ReflectionColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat6.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz / u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.01900005, 1.01900005, 1.01900005);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.20000005, 2.20000005, 2.20000005);
    SV_Target0.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    return;
}

#define HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS 1
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
#define UNITY_UNIFORM
#else
#define UNITY_UNIFORM uniform
#endif
#define UNITY_SUPPORTS_UNIFORM_LOCATION 1
#if UNITY_SUPPORTS_UNIFORM_LOCATION
#define UNITY_LOCATION(x) layout(location = x)
#define UNITY_BINDING(x) layout(binding = x, std140)
#else
#define UNITY_LOCATION(x)
#define UNITY_BINDING(x) layout(std140)
#endif
uniform 	float _Offset;
uniform 	vec4 _MainLightPosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainLightColor;
uniform 	vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;
uniform 	vec4 _ProjectionParams;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[20];
uniform 	mediump vec4 _DarkCorner;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainHighLightOffset;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(0) uniform UnityPerDraw {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[4];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_LODFade;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_WorldTransformParams;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_LightData;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_LightIndices[2];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_ProbesOcclusion;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_LightmapST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_DynamicLightmapST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAr;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAg;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAb;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBr;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBg;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBb;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHC;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(1) uniform UnityPerMaterial {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RoughNessOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _UVScallePaner;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cutoff;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _NormalStrong;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _IFMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RenderType;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cull;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ZWrite;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ZTest;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _AlphaToMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SrcBlendFactor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DstBlendFactor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SrcBlendFactorAlpha;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DstBlendFactorAlpha;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _BlendOp;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _BlendOpAlpha;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EmissColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MetallicOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _IFEmiss;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _GlobalLightEmiss;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _LocalLightOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _ReflectionColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec3 _ReflectionOffset;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD10;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD11;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD12;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump float u_xlat16_10;
float u_xlat18;
mediump float u_xlat16_22;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _UVScallePaner.xy + _UVScallePaner.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.w = 0.0;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.z = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    vs_TEXCOORD0.z = min(max(vs_TEXCOORD0.z, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    vs_TEXCOORD0.z = clamp(vs_TEXCOORD0.z, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat3.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat3.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _MainHighLightOffset.xyz + _LocalLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_22) + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_3;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat5.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat5.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat5.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.xzw = u_xlat16_4.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_10)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat2.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_4.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_4.z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + (-_ReflectionOffset.xyz);
    u_xlat2 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat2 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat2;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat2;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat0.y = u_xlat0.y * _ProjectionParams.x;
    u_xlat2.xzw = u_xlat0.xwy * vec3(0.5, 0.5, 0.5);
    vs_TEXCOORD12.zw = u_xlat0.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD12.xy = u_xlat2.zz + u_xlat2.xw;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat1.x = _Offset * 0.00999999978;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x / u_xlat0.w;
    gl_Position.z = u_xlat0.z + (-u_xlat1.x);
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat0.xyw;
    return;
}

#endif

precision highp float;
precision highp int;

uniform 	vec4 _EnvScale;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainLightShadowParams;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _GISpecularColor;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _GIDiffuseColor;

#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _ReflectionTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(5) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD12;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
vec3 u_xlat6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
vec3 u_xlat8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
bool u_xlatb9;
mediump float u_xlat16_10;
vec3 u_xlat15;
mediump float u_xlat16_19;
float u_xlat24;
mediump float u_xlat16_28;
void main()
{
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(vs_TEXCOORD7.xy,vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
    u_xlat16_0.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_1.x = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_1.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb9 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb9 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlatb9 || u_xlatb0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_10 = _NormalStrong;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_10 = min(max(u_xlat16_10, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_10 = clamp(u_xlat16_10, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_10) * u_xlat16_3.xy;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_4.y = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_4.z = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_10 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_10 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_10);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_10) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_0.y * 0.5 + 0.75;
    u_xlat16_10 = max(u_xlat16_10, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_10 = min(u_xlat16_10, 1.25);
    u_xlat16_19 = (-u_xlat16_10) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_19 + u_xlat16_10;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat16_0.y * u_xlat16_0.y;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat16_0.x * u_xlat16_0.x + (-u_xlat16_19);
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_0.yzzx * u_xlat16_0.xyzz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(unity_SHBr, u_xlat16_2);
    u_xlat16_3.y = dot(unity_SHBg, u_xlat16_2);
    u_xlat16_3.z = dot(unity_SHBb, u_xlat16_2);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = unity_SHC.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_19) + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.w = 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(unity_SHAr, u_xlat16_0);
    u_xlat16_4.y = dot(unity_SHAg, u_xlat16_0);
    u_xlat16_4.z = dot(unity_SHAb, u_xlat16_0);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = max(u_xlat16_3.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat16_2.x + _MetallicOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_19 = min(max(u_xlat16_19, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_19 = clamp(u_xlat16_19, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_4 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = (-u_xlat16_4.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_19) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_10) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat6.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat6.x = min(max(u_xlat6.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat6.x = clamp(u_xlat6.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat15.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat15.x = min(max(u_xlat15.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else

    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat10_6.xyz * vec3(4.84000015, 4.84000015, 4.84000015);
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_27 * u_xlat16_17 + u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = u_xlat16_13.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xxx * u_xlat16_13.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_27) + u_xlat16_13.xyz;
    u_xlat16_13.x = dot((-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_13.x = u_xlat16_13.x + u_xlat16_13.x;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-u_xlat16_13.xxx) + (-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_13.x = (-u_xlat16_31) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_31 * u_xlat16_13.x;
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_31 * 6.0;
    u_xlat10_1 = textureCube(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_31);
    u_xlat16_13.x = u_xlat10_1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_13.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_13.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_13.x = max(u_xlat16_13.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_13.x = log2(u_xlat16_13.x);
    u_xlat16_13.x = u_xlat16_13.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_13.x = exp2(u_xlat16_13.x);
    u_xlat16_13.x = u_xlat16_13.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * u_xlat16_13.xxx;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_13.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xxx;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * _EnvScale.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat10_2.w * _IFEmiss;
    u_xlat16_13.x = sqrt(u_xlat10_2.z);
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat10_4.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xxx;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat10_4.w + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = _IFMask * u_xlat16_7.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_3.xzw * _EmissColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_13.xxx + u_xlat16_3.xzw;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat2.xy = vs_TEXCOORD12.xy / vs_TEXCOORD12.ww;
    u_xlat10_2.xyz = texture2D(_ReflectionTex, u_xlat2.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat10_2.xyz * _ReflectionColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz / u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(1.01900005, 1.01900005, 1.01900005);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.20000005, 2.20000005, 2.20000005);
    SV_Target0.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    return;
}

    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_4.z = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_10 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_10 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_10);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_10) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_0.y * 0.5 + 0.75;
    u_xlat16_10 = max(u_xlat16_10, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_10 = min(u_xlat16_10, 1.25);
    u_xlat16_19 = (-u_xlat16_10) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_19 + u_xlat16_10;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat16_0.y * u_xlat16_0.y;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat16_0.x * u_xlat16_0.x + (-u_xlat16_19);
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_0.yzzx * u_xlat16_0.xyzz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(unity_SHBr, u_xlat16_2);
    u_xlat16_3.y = dot(unity_SHBg, u_xlat16_2);
    u_xlat16_3.z = dot(unity_SHBb, u_xlat16_2);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = unity_SHC.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_19) + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.w = 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(unity_SHAr, u_xlat16_0);
    u_xlat16_4.y = dot(unity_SHAg, u_xlat16_0);
    u_xlat16_4.z = dot(unity_SHAb, u_xlat16_0);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = max(u_xlat16_3.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat10_2 = texture2D(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat10_2.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_19 = clamp(u_xlat16_19, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10_4 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = (-u_xlat10_4.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_19) + u_xlat10_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_10) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat6.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat6.x = clamp(u_xlat6.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat15.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat15.x = clamp(u_xlat15.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat24 = (-u_xlat15.x) * u_xlat15.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat10_2.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_10 = clamp(u_xlat16_10, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_10 * u_xlat16_10;
    u_xlat15.x = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat15.x;
    u_xlat15.x = u_xlat15.x * u_xlat15.x + u_xlat24;
    u_xlat15.x = max(u_xlat15.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat15.x = u_xlat16_28 / u_xlat15.x;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_28 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_28 = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat15.x = u_xlat15.x * u_xlat15.x;
    u_xlat24 = u_xlat16_10 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat15.x = u_xlat15.x * u_xlat24;
    u_xlat15.x = min(u_xlat15.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat10_4.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_19) * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat15.xyz = u_xlat15.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat15.xyz = u_xlat6.xxx * u_xlat15.xyz;
    u_xlat15.xyz = u_xlat15.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat15.xyz = u_xlat15.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat15.xyz;
    u_xlat8.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat8.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat8.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xxx + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot((-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz), u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x + u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * (-u_xlat16_1.xxx) + (-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = (-u_xlat16_10) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_10;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * 6.0;
    u_xlat10_0 = textureCube(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat10_0.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_1.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_1.x = log2(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_1.x = exp2(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xxx;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat8.xyz * _EnvScale.xyz + u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat10_2.w * _IFEmiss;
    u_xlat16_10 = sqrt(u_xlat10_2.z);
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = u_xlat10_4.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xxx;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat10_4.w + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = _IFMask * u_xlat16_3.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = u_xlat16_1.xzw * _EmissColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_10) + u_xlat16_1.xzw;
    u_xlat6.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat6.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat6.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat8.xy = vs_TEXCOORD12.xy / vs_TEXCOORD12.ww;
    u_xlat10_8.xyz = texture2D(_ReflectionTex, u_xlat8.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat10_8.xyz * _ReflectionColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat6.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.20000005, 2.20000005, 2.20000005);
    return;
}

    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat2;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat0.y = u_xlat0.y * _ProjectionParams.x;
    u_xlat2.xzw = u_xlat0.xwy * vec3(0.5, 0.5, 0.5);
    vs_TEXCOORD12.zw = u_xlat0.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD12.xy = u_xlat2.zz + u_xlat2.xw;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat1.x = _Offset * 0.00999999978;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x / u_xlat0.w;
    gl_Position.z = u_xlat0.z + (-u_xlat1.x);
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat0.xyw;
    return;
}

    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);

#else

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat10.x = min(max(u_xlat10.x, 0.0), 1.0);

    u_xlat16_7.x = min(u_xlat16_7.x, 1.25);
    u_xlat16_17 = (-u_xlat16_7.x) + 1.0;

    u_xlat16_13.x = u_xlat16_13.x + u_xlat16_13.x;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-u_xlat16_13.xxx) + (-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_13.x = (-u_xlat16_31) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_31 * u_xlat16_13.x;

    SV_Target0.w = _IFMask * u_xlat16_7.x + 1.0;

    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;

{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;

	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_ProbesOcclusion;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_LightmapST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_DynamicLightmapST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAr;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAg;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAb;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBr;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHC;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(1) uniform UnityPerMaterial {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RoughNessOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _UVScallePaner;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cutoff;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _NormalStrong;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _IFMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RenderType;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cull;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ZWrite;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ZTest;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _AlphaToMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SrcBlendFactor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DstBlendFactor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SrcBlendFactorAlpha;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DstBlendFactorAlpha;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _BlendOp;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _BlendOpAlpha;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EmissColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MetallicOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _IFEmiss;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _GlobalLightEmiss;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
float u_xlat6;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _LightDirection.xyz * _ShadowBias.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat6 = dot(_LightDirection.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat6 = min(max(u_xlat6, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat6 = (-u_xlat6) + 1.0;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat6 * _ShadowBias.y;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat6) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position.z = max((-u_xlat0.w), u_xlat0.z);
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat0.xyw;
    return;
}

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
#version 300 es

precision highp float;
precision highp int;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_TARGET0;
void main()
{
    SV_TARGET0 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

#endif
"
}
